I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Stacked charts with irregular time intervals interpolate incorrectly
## Description

Stacked area charts with irregular time points where some time series have values for all time points and other only for some interpolate without taking the spacing of the time points into account.

## Expected behaviour

When doing linear interpolation across a longer time span with irregularly placed time points, interpolation should work correctly.

## Steps to reproduce

Steps to reproduce the behavior:

1. Open the literacy rate chart in the admin: https://admin.owid.io/admin/charts/2617/edit
2. Change the chart type to stacked area
3. Select only Germany. Between 1750 and 1950, no real values exist.
4. Add France, which has additional values between 1900 and 1950. 
5. Observe that Germany shows a upwards sloping curve - the reason is that the 8 additional points are calculated as if they were spaced evenly (each incrementing by the same amount) even though they are not spaced evenly in time.

## Screenshots

<img width="807" height="570" alt="Image" src="https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/4c89bbb9-1b24-4752-a161-7af1da56d734" />


</pr_description>

     1	import * as _ from "lodash-es"
     2	import {
     3	    sortNumeric,
     4	    isArrayOfNumbers,
     5	    findGreatestCommonDivisorOfArray,
     6	    rollingMap,
     7	    omitUndefinedValues,
     8	} from "@ourworldindata/utils"
     9	import { StackedPointPositionType, StackedSeries } from "./StackedConstants"
    10	
    11	// This method shift up the Y Values of a Series with Points in place.
    12	export const stackSeries = <PositionType extends StackedPointPositionType>(
    13	    seriesArr: readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[]
    14	): readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[] => {
    15	    seriesArr.forEach((series, seriesIndex) => {
    16	        if (!seriesIndex) return // The first series does not need to be shifted
    17	        series.points.forEach((point, pointIndex) => {
    18	            const pointBelowThisOne =
    19	                seriesArr[seriesIndex - 1].points[pointIndex]
    20	            point.valueOffset =
    21	                pointBelowThisOne.value + pointBelowThisOne.valueOffset
    22	        })
    23	    })
    24	    return seriesArr
    25	}
    26	
    27	// This method shifts up positive y values and shifts down negative y values of a Series with Points in place.
    28	export const stackSeriesInBothDirections = <
    29	    PositionType extends StackedPointPositionType,
    30	>(
    31	    seriesArr: readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[]
    32	): readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[] => {
    33	    seriesArr.forEach((series, seriesIndex) => {
    34	        if (!seriesIndex) return // The first series does not need to be shifted
    35	        series.points.forEach((point, pointIndex) => {
    36	            const pointsBelowThisOne = seriesArr
    37	                .slice(0, seriesIndex)
    38	                .map((s) => s.points[pointIndex])
    39	            const pointBelowThisOne =
    40	                point.value < 0
    41	                    ? pointsBelowThisOne.findLast((p) => p.value < 0)
    42	                    : pointsBelowThisOne.findLast((p) => p.value >= 0)
    43	            point.valueOffset = pointBelowThisOne
    44	                ? pointBelowThisOne.value + pointBelowThisOne.valueOffset
    45	                : 0
    46	        })
    47	    })
    48	    return seriesArr
    49	}
    50	
    51	// Makes sure that values are evenly spaced
    52	export function withUniformSpacing(values: number[]): number[] {
    53	    const deltas = rollingMap(values, (a, b) => b - a)
    54	    const gcd = findGreatestCommonDivisorOfArray(deltas)
    55	    if (gcd === null) return values
    56	    return _.range(values[0], values[values.length - 1] + gcd, gcd)
    57	}
    58	
    59	// Adds a Y = 0 value for each missing x value (where X is usually Time)
    60	export const withMissingValuesAsZeroes = <
    61	    PositionType extends StackedPointPositionType,
    62	>(
    63	    seriesArr: readonly StackedSeries<PositionType>[],
    64	    { enforceUniformSpacing = false }: { enforceUniformSpacing?: boolean } = {}
    65	): StackedSeries<PositionType>[] => {
    66	    let allXValuesSorted = sortNumeric(
    67	        _.uniq(
    68	            seriesArr
    69	                .flatMap((series) => series.points)
    70	                .map((point) => point.position)
    71	        )
    72	    )
    73	
    74	    if (enforceUniformSpacing && isArrayOfNumbers(allXValuesSorted)) {
    75	        allXValuesSorted = withUniformSpacing(
    76	            allXValuesSorted
    77	        ) as PositionType[]
    78	    }
    79	
    80	    return seriesArr.map((series) => {
    81	        const pointsByPosition = _.keyBy(series.points, "position")
    82	        return {
    83	            ...series,
    84	            points: allXValuesSorted.map((position) => {
    85	                const point = pointsByPosition[position]
    86	                const value = point?.value ?? 0
    87	                const time = point?.time ?? 0
    88	                return omitUndefinedValues({
    89	                    time,
    90	                    position,
    91	                    value,
    92	                    valueOffset: 0,
    93	                    interpolated: point?.interpolated,
    94	                    fake: !point || !!point.interpolated,
    95	                    color: point?.color,
    96	                })
    97	            }),
    98	        }
    99	    })
   100	}

    69	    transformTable(table: OwidTable): OwidTable {
    70	        table = table.filterByEntityNames(
    71	            this.selectionArray.selectedEntityNames
    72	        )
    73	
    74	        // TODO: remove this filter once we don't have mixed type columns in datasets
    75	        table = table
    76	            .replaceNonNumericCellsWithErrorValues(this.yColumnSlugs)
    77	            .dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAllColumns(this.yColumnSlugs)
    78	
    79	        if (this.shouldRunLinearInterpolation) {
    80	            this.yColumnSlugs.forEach((slug) => {
    81	                table = table.interpolateColumnLinearly(slug)
    82	            })
    83	        }
    84	
    85	        // Drop rows for which no valid data points exist for any display column
    86	        // after interpolation, which most likely means they lie at the start/end
    87	        // of the time range and were not extrapolated
    88	        if (this.missingDataStrategy !== MissingDataStrategy.show) {
    89	            table = table.dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAnyColumn(this.yColumnSlugs)
    90	        }
    91	
    92	        if (this.manager.isRelativeMode) {
    93	            table = this.isEntitySeries
    94	                ? table.toPercentageFromEachEntityForEachTime(
    95	                      this.yColumnSlugs[0]
    96	                  )
    97	                : table.toPercentageFromEachColumnForEachEntityAndTime(
    98	                      this.yColumnSlugs
    99	                  )
   100	        }
   101	        return table
   102	    }
   103	
   104	    transformTableForSelection(table: OwidTable): OwidTable {
   105	        // if entities with partial data are not plotted,
   106	        // make sure they don't show up in the entity selector
   107	        if (this.missingDataStrategy !== MissingDataStrategy.show) {
   108	            table = table
   109	                .replaceNonNumericCellsWithErrorValues(this.yColumnSlugs)
   110	                .dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAllColumns(this.yColumnSlugs)
   111	
   112	            if (this.shouldRunLinearInterpolation) {
   113	                this.yColumnSlugs.forEach((slug) => {
   114	                    table = table.interpolateColumnLinearly(slug)
   115	                })
   116	            }
   117	
   118	            table = table.dropRowsWithErrorValuesForAnyColumn(this.yColumnSlugs)
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        return table
   122	    }

   295	            })
   296	            .toReversed() // For stacked charts, we want the first selected series to be on top, so we reverse the order of the stacks.

   298	
   299	    @computed
   300	    private get entitiesAsSeries(): readonly StackedRawSeries<number>[] {
   301	        if (!this.yColumns.length) return []
   302	
   303	        const { isProjection, owidRowsByEntityName } = this.yColumns[0]
   304	        return this.selectionArray.selectedEntityNames
   305	            .map((seriesName) => {
   306	                return {
   307	                    isProjection,
   308	                    seriesName,
   309	                    rows: owidRowsByEntityName.get(seriesName) || [],
   310	                }
   311	            })
   312	            .toReversed() // For stacked charts, we want the first selected series to be on top, so we reverse the order of the stacks.
   313	    }

   341	    @computed private get categoricalColorAssigner(): CategoricalColorAssigner {
   342	        const seriesCount = this.isEntitySeries
   343	            ? this.selectionArray.numSelectedEntities
   344	            : this.yColumns.length
   345	        return new CategoricalColorAssigner({
   346	            colorScheme:
   347	                (this.manager.baseColorScheme
   348	                    ? ColorSchemes.get(this.manager.baseColorScheme)
   349	                    : null) ??
   350	                ColorSchemes.get(ColorSchemeName.stackedAreaDefault),
   351	            invertColorScheme: this.manager.invertColorScheme,
   352	            colorMap: this.colorMap,
   353	            autoColorMapCache: this.manager.seriesColorMap,
   354	            numColorsInUse: seriesCount,
   355	        })
   356	    }

   359	        return makeSelectionArray(this.manager.selection)
   360	    }
   361	
   362	    @computed get isEntitySeries(): boolean {
   363	        return this.seriesStrategy === SeriesStrategy.entity
   364	    }
   365	
   366	    @computed get seriesColors(): string[] {
   367	        return this.series.map((series) => series.color)
   368	    }
   369	
   370	    @computed get availableFacetStrategies(): FacetStrategy[] {
   371	        const strategies: FacetStrategy[] = []
   372	
   373	        const { selectedEntityNames } = this.selectionArray
   374	        const areMultipleEntitiesSelected = selectedEntityNames.length > 1
   375	        const hasMultipleYColumns = this.yColumns.length > 1
   376	        const shortUnits = this.yColumns.map((column) => column.shortUnit)
   377	        const uniqueUnits = new Set(shortUnits)
   378	        const hasMultipleUnits = uniqueUnits.size > 1
   379	        const hasPercentageUnit = shortUnits.some(
   380	            (shortUnit) => shortUnit === "%"
   381	        )
   382	
   383	        // Normally StackedArea/StackedBar charts are always single-entity or single-column,
   384	        // but if we are ever in a mode where we have multiple entities selected (e.g. through
   385	        // GlobalEntitySelector) and multiple columns, it only makes sense when faceted.
   386	        if (
   387	            // No facet strategy makes sense if columns are stacked and a single entity is selected
   388	            (!this.isEntitySeries && !areMultipleEntitiesSelected) ||
   389	            // No facet strategy makes sense if entities are stacked and we have a single column
   390	            (this.isEntitySeries &&
   391	                !hasMultipleYColumns &&
   392	                // The stacking must be sensible
   393	                checkIsStackingEntitiesSensible(selectedEntityNames))
   394	        )
   395	            strategies.push(FacetStrategy.none)
   396	
   397	        if (
   398	            // Facetting by entity makes sense if multiple entities are selected
   399	            areMultipleEntitiesSelected &&
   400	            // Stacking columns with different units isn't allowed
   401	            !hasMultipleUnits
   402	        )
   403	            strategies.push(FacetStrategy.entity)
   404	
   405	        if (
   406	            // Facetting by column makes sense if we have multiple columns
   407	            hasMultipleYColumns &&
   408	            // Stacking percentages doesn't make sense unless we're in relative mode
   409	            (!hasPercentageUnit || this.manager.isRelativeMode) &&
   410	            // Some stacked entity combinations are not allowed, e.g. stacking
   411	            // countries on top their continent or stacking countries or continents
   412	            // on top of World
   413	            checkIsStackingEntitiesSensible(selectedEntityNames)
   414	        )
   415	            strategies.push(FacetStrategy.metric)
   416	
   417	        return strategies
   418	    }
   419	
   420	    @computed get shouldUseValueBasedColorScheme(): boolean {
   421	        return false
   422	    }
   423	
   424	    @computed get useValueBasedColorScheme(): boolean {
   425	        return false
   426	    }
   427	
   428	    @computed get unstackedSeries(): readonly StackedSeries<number>[] {
   429	        return this.rawSeries
   430	            .filter((series) => series.rows.length > 0)
   431	
   432	            .map((series) => {
   433	                const { isProjection, seriesName, rows } = series
   434	
   435	                const points = rows.map((row) => {
   436	                    const pointColor =
   437	                        row.value > 0 ? POSITIVE_COLOR : NEGATIVE_COLOR
   438	                    return {
   439	                        position: row.originalTime,
   440	                        time: row.originalTime,
   441	                        value: row.value,
   442	                        valueOffset: 0,
   443	                        interpolated:
   444	                            this.shouldRunLinearInterpolation &&
   445	                            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(row.value) &&
   446	                            !isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(row.originalValue),
   447	                        // takes precedence over the series color if given
   448	                        color: this.useValueBasedColorScheme
   449	                            ? pointColor
   450	                            : undefined,
   451	                    }
   452	                })
   453	
   454	                return {
   455	                    seriesName,
   456	                    isProjection,
   457	                    points,
   458	                    isAllZeros: points.every((point) => point.value === 0),
   459	                    color: this.categoricalColorAssigner.assign(seriesName),
   460	                }
   461	            }) as StackedSeries<number>[]
   462	    }

    63	
    64	const AREA_OPACITY = {
    65	    default: GRAPHER_AREA_OPACITY_DEFAULT,
    66	    focus: GRAPHER_AREA_OPACITY_FOCUS,
    67	    mute: GRAPHER_AREA_OPACITY_MUTE,
    68	} as const
    69	
    70	const BORDER_OPACITY = {
    71	    default: 0.7,
    72	    focus: 1,
    73	    mute: 0.3,
    74	} as const
    75	
    76	const BORDER_WIDTH = {
    77	    default: 0.5,
    78	    focus: 1.5,
    79	} as const
    80	
    81	@observer
    82	class Areas extends React.Component<AreasProps> {
    83	    @bind placePoint(point: StackedPoint<number>): StackedPlacedPoint {
    84	        const { dualAxis } = this.props
    85	        const { horizontalAxis, verticalAxis } = dualAxis
    86	        return [
    87	            horizontalAxis.place(point.position),
    88	            verticalAxis.place(point.value + point.valueOffset),
    89	        ]
    90	    }
    91	
    92	    // This places a whole series, but the points only represent the top of the area.
    93	    // Later steps are necessary to display them as a filled area.
    94	    @bind placeSeries(
    95	        series: StackedSeries<number>
    96	    ): Array<StackedPlacedPoint> {
    97	        const { dualAxis } = this.props
    98	        const { horizontalAxis, verticalAxis } = dualAxis
    99	
   100	        if (series.points.length > 1) {
   101	            return series.points.map(this.placePoint)
   102	        } else if (series.points.length === 1) {
   103	            // We only have one point, so make it so it stretches out over the whole x axis range
   104	            // There are two cases here that we need to consider:
   105	            // (1) In unfaceted charts, the x domain will be a single year, so we need to ensure that the area stretches
   106	            //     out over the full range of the x axis.
   107	            // (2) In faceted charts, the x domain may span multiple years, so we need to ensure that the area stretches
   108	            //     out only over year - 0.5 to year + 0.5, additionally making sure we don't put points outside the x range.
   109	            //
   110	            // -@marcelgerber, 2023-04-24
   111	            const point = series.points[0]
   112	            const y = verticalAxis.place(point.value + point.valueOffset)
   113	            const singleValueXDomain =
   114	                horizontalAxis.domain[0] === horizontalAxis.domain[1]
   115	
   116	            if (singleValueXDomain) {
   117	                // Case (1)
   118	                return [
   119	                    [horizontalAxis.range[0], y],
   120	                    [horizontalAxis.range[1], y],
   121	                ]
   122	            } else {
   123	                // Case (2)
   124	                const leftX = Math.max(
   125	                    horizontalAxis.place(point.position - 0.5),
   126	                    horizontalAxis.range[0]
   127	                )
   128	                const rightX = Math.min(
   129	                    horizontalAxis.place(point.position + 0.5),
   130	                    horizontalAxis.range[1]
   131	                )
   132	
   133	                return [
   134	                    [leftX, y],
   135	                    [rightX, y],
   136	                ]
   137	            }
   138	        } else return []
   139	    }
   140	
   141	    @computed get placedSeriesArr(): StackedPlacedSeries<number>[] {
   142	        const { seriesArr } = this.props
   143	        return seriesArr
   144	            .filter((series) => !series.isAllZeros)
   145	            .map((series) => ({
   146	                ...series,
   147	                placedPoints: this.placeSeries(series),
   148	            }))
   149	    }
   150	
   151	    @computed get isFocusModeActive(): boolean {
   152	        return this.props.focusedSeriesName !== undefined
   153	    }
   154	
   155	    @computed private get areas(): React.ReactElement[] {
   156	        const { placedSeriesArr } = this
   157	        const { dualAxis, focusedSeriesName } = this.props
   158	        const { verticalAxis } = dualAxis
   159	
   160	        return placedSeriesArr.map((series, index) => {
   161	            const { placedPoints } = series
   162	            let prevPoints: Array<StackedPlacedPoint>
   163	            if (index > 0) {
   164	                prevPoints = placedSeriesArr[index - 1].placedPoints
   165	            } else {
   166	                prevPoints = [
   167	                    [
   168	                        placedPoints[0][0], // placed x coord of first (= leftmost) point in chart
   169	                        verticalAxis.range[0],
   170	                    ],
   171	                    [
   172	                        lastOfNonEmptyArray(placedPoints)[0], // placed x coord of last (= rightmost) point in chart
   173	                        verticalAxis.range[0],
   174	                    ],
   175	                ]
   176	            }
   177	            const points = [...placedPoints, ...prevPoints.toReversed()]
   178	            const opacity = !this.isFocusModeActive
   179	                ? AREA_OPACITY.default // normal opacity
   180	                : focusedSeriesName === series.seriesName
   181	                  ? AREA_OPACITY.focus // hovered
   182	                  : AREA_OPACITY.mute // non-hovered
   183	
   184	            return (
   185	                <path
   186	                    id={makeIdForHumanConsumption(series.seriesName)}
   187	                    className={makeSafeForCSS(series.seriesName) + "-area"}
   188	                    key={series.seriesName + "-area"}
   189	                    strokeLinecap="round"
   190	                    d={pointsToPath(points)}
   191	                    fill={series.color}
   192	                    fillOpacity={opacity}
   193	                    clipPath={this.props.clipPath}
   194	                    onMouseEnter={(): void => {
   195	                        this.props.onAreaMouseEnter?.(series.seriesName)
   196	                    }}
   197	                    onMouseLeave={(): void => {
   198	                        this.props.onAreaMouseLeave?.()
   199	                    }}
   200	                />
   201	            )
   202	        })
   203	    }
   204	
   205	    @computed private get borders(): React.ReactElement[] {
   206	        const { placedSeriesArr } = this
   207	        const { focusedSeriesName } = this.props
   208	
   209	        return placedSeriesArr.map((placedSeries) => {
   210	            const opacity = !this.isFocusModeActive
   211	                ? BORDER_OPACITY.default // normal opacity
   212	                : focusedSeriesName === placedSeries.seriesName
   213	                  ? BORDER_OPACITY.focus // hovered
   214	                  : BORDER_OPACITY.mute // non-hovered
   215	            const strokeWidth =
   216	                focusedSeriesName === placedSeries.seriesName
   217	                    ? BORDER_WIDTH.focus
   218	                    : BORDER_WIDTH.default
   219	
   220	            return (
   221	                <path
   222	                    id={makeIdForHumanConsumption(placedSeries.seriesName)}
   223	                    className={
   224	                        makeSafeForCSS(placedSeries.seriesName) + "-border"
   225	                    }
   226	                    key={placedSeries.seriesName + "-border"}
   227	                    strokeLinecap="round"
   228	                    d={pointsToPath(placedSeries.placedPoints)}
   229	                    stroke={rgb(placedSeries.color).darker(0.5).toString()}
   230	                    strokeOpacity={opacity}
   231	                    strokeWidth={strokeWidth}
   232	                    fill="none"
   233	                    clipPath={this.props.clipPath}
   234	                    onMouseEnter={(): void => {
   235	                        this.props.onAreaMouseEnter?.(placedSeries.seriesName)
   236	                    }}
   237	                    onMouseLeave={(): void => {
   238	                        this.props.onAreaMouseLeave?.()
   239	                    }}
   240	                />
   241	            )
   242	        })
   243	    }
   244	
   245	    render(): React.ReactElement {
   246	        return (
   247	            <g
   248	                className="Areas"
   249	                id={makeIdForHumanConsumption("stacked-areas")}
   250	            >
   251	                <g id={makeIdForHumanConsumption("areas")}>{this.areas}</g>
   252	                <g id={makeIdForHumanConsumption("borders")}>{this.borders}</g>
   253	            </g>
   254	        )
   255	    }
   256	}
   257	
   258	@observer
   259	export class StackedAreaChart extends AbstractStackedChart {
   260	    constructor(props: AbstractStackedChartProps) {
   261	        super(props)
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    @computed protected get yAxisDomain(): [number, number] {
   265	        const yValues = this.allStackedPoints.map(
   266	            (point) => point.value + point.valueOffset
   267	        )
   268	        return [0, _.max(yValues) ?? 0]
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    @computed protected get xAxisConfig(): AxisConfig {
   272	        return new AxisConfig(
   273	            {
   274	                hideGridlines: true,
   275	                ...this.manager.xAxisConfig,
   276	            },
   277	            this
   278	        )
   279	    }
   280	
   281	    @computed get midpoints(): number[] {
   282	        let prevY = 0
   283	        return this.series.map((series) => {
   284	            const lastValue = R.last(series.points)
   285	            if (!lastValue) return 0
   286	
   287	            const y = lastValue.value + lastValue.valueOffset
   288	            const middleY = prevY + (y - prevY) / 2
   289	            prevY = y
   290	            return middleY
   291	        })
   292	    }
   293	
   294	    private hoverStateForSeries(
   295	        series: StackedSeries<number>
   296	    ): InteractionState {
   297	        return getHoverStateForSeries(series, {
   298	            isHoverModeActive: this.isHoverModeActive,
   299	            hoveredSeriesNames: this.hoveredSeriesNames,
   300	        })
   301	    }
   302	
   303	    @computed get lineLegendSeries(): LineLabelSeries[] {
   304	        const { midpoints } = this
   305	        return this.series
   306	            .map((series, index) => ({
   307	                color: series.color,
   308	                seriesName: series.seriesName,
   309	                label: series.seriesName,
   310	                yValue: midpoints[index],
   311	                isAllZeros: series.isAllZeros,
   312	                hover: this.hoverStateForSeries(series),
   313	            }))
   314	            .filter((series) => !series.isAllZeros)
   315	            .toReversed()
   316	    }
   317	
   318	    @computed get maxLineLegendWidth(): number {
   319	        return Math.min(150, this.bounds.width / 3)
   320	    }
   321	
   322	    @computed get lineLegendWidth(): number {
   323	        if (!this.manager.showLegend) return 0
   324	
   325	        // only pass props that are required to calculate
   326	        // the width to avoid circular dependencies
   327	        return LineLegend.stableWidth({
   328	            series: this.lineLegendSeries,
   329	            maxWidth: this.maxLineLegendWidth,
   330	            fontSize: this.fontSize,
   331	        })
   332	    }
   333	
   334	    @observable tooltipState = new TooltipState<{
   335	        index: number // time-index into points array
   336	        series?: SeriesName
   337	    }>({ fade: "immediate" })
   338	
   339	    @action.bound private onAreaMouseEnter(seriesName: SeriesName): void {
   340	        if (this.tooltipState.target) {
   341	            _.extend(this.tooltipState.target, { series: seriesName })
   342	        } else {
   343	            this.tooltipState.target = {
   344	                index: 0, // might be incorrect but will be updated immediately by the move event handler
   345	                series: seriesName,
   346	            }
   347	        }
   348	    }
   349	
   350	    @action.bound private onAreaMouseLeave(): void {
   351	        _.extend(this.tooltipState.target, { series: undefined })
   352	    }
   353	
   354	    @observable lineLegendHoveredSeriesName?: SeriesName
   355	    @observable private hoverTimer?: NodeJS.Timeout
   356	
   357	    @computed protected get paddingForLegendRight(): number {
   358	        return this.lineLegendWidth
   359	    }
   360	
   361	    @computed get seriesSortedByImportance(): string[] {
   362	        return this.series
   363	            .toSorted(
   364	                (
   365	                    s1: StackedSeries<number>,
   366	                    s2: StackedSeries<number>
   367	                ): number => {
   368	                    const PREFER_S1 = -1
   369	                    const PREFER_S2 = 1
   370	
   371	                    if (!s1) return PREFER_S2
   372	                    if (!s2) return PREFER_S1
   373	
   374	                    // early return if one series is all zeroes
   375	                    if (s1.isAllZeros && !s2.isAllZeros) return PREFER_S2
   376	                    if (s2.isAllZeros && !s1.isAllZeros) return PREFER_S1
   377	
   378	                    // prefer series with a higher maximum value
   379	                    const yMax1 = _.maxBy(s1.points, (p) => p.value)?.value ?? 0
   380	                    const yMax2 = _.maxBy(s2.points, (p) => p.value)?.value ?? 0
   381	                    if (yMax1 > yMax2) return PREFER_S1
   382	                    if (yMax2 > yMax1) return PREFER_S2
   383	
   384	                    // prefer series with a higher last value
   385	                    const yLast1 = R.last(s1.points)?.value ?? 0
   386	                    const yLast2 = R.last(s2.points)?.value ?? 0
   387	                    if (yLast1 > yLast2) return PREFER_S1
   388	                    if (yLast2 > yLast1) return PREFER_S2
   389	
   390	                    // prefer series with a higher total area
   391	                    const area1 = _.sumBy(s1.points, (p) => p.value)
   392	                    const area2 = _.sumBy(s2.points, (p) => p.value)
   393	                    if (area1 > area2) return PREFER_S1
   394	                    if (area2 > area1) return PREFER_S2
   395	
   396	                    return 0
   397	                }
   398	            )
   399	            .map((s) => s.seriesName)
   400	    }
   401	
   402	    @action.bound onLineLegendMouseOver(seriesName: SeriesName): void {
   403	        clearTimeout(this.hoverTimer)
   404	        this.lineLegendHoveredSeriesName = seriesName
   405	    }
   406	
   407	    @action.bound onLineLegendMouseLeave(): void {
   408	        clearTimeout(this.hoverTimer)
   409	        this.hoverTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   410	            // wait before clearing selection in case the mouse is moving quickly over neighboring labels
   411	            this.lineLegendHoveredSeriesName = undefined
   412	        }, 200)
   413	    }
   414	
   415	    @computed get facetLegendHoveredSeriesName(): SeriesName | undefined {
   416	        const { externalLegendHoverBin } = this.manager
   417	        if (!externalLegendHoverBin) return undefined
   418	        // stacked area charts can't plot the same entity or column multiple times,
   419	        // so we just find the first series that matches the hovered legend item
   420	        const hoveredSeries = this.rawSeries.find((series) =>
   421	            externalLegendHoverBin.contains(series.seriesName)
   422	        )
   423	        return hoveredSeries?.seriesName
   424	    }
   425	
   426	    @computed get hoveredSeriesName(): SeriesName | undefined {
   427	        return (
   428	            // if the chart area is hovered
   429	            this.tooltipState.target?.series ??
   430	            // if the line legend is hovered
   431	            this.lineLegendHoveredSeriesName ?? // if the facet legend is hovered
   432	            this.facetLegendHoveredSeriesName
   433	        )
   434	    }
   435	
   436	    @computed get isHoverModeActive(): boolean {
   437	        return (
   438	            !!this.hoveredSeriesName ||
   439	            // if the external legend is hovered, we want to mute

   124	    filterByEntityNames(names: EntityName[]): this {

   133	    filterByEntityNamesUsingIncludeExcludePattern({
   134	        excluded,
   135	        included,
   136	    }: {
   137	        excluded?: EntityName[]
   138	        included?: EntityName[]
   139	    }): this {
   140	        if (!included && !excluded) return this
   141	
   142	        const excludedSet = new Set(excluded)
   143	        const includedSet = new Set(included)
   144	
   145	        const excludeFilter = (entityName: EntityName): boolean =>
   146	            !excludedSet.has(entityName)
   147	        const includeFilter =
   148	            includedSet.size > 0
   149	                ? (entityName: EntityName): boolean =>
   150	                      includedSet.has(entityName)
   151	                : (): boolean => true
   152	
   153	        const filterFn = (entityName: any): boolean =>
   154	            excludeFilter(entityName) && includeFilter(entityName)

   156	        const excludedList = excluded ? excluded.join(", ") : ""
   157	        const includedList = included ? included.join(", ") : ""
   158	
   159	        return this.columnFilter(
   160	            this.entityNameSlug,
   161	            filterFn,
   162	            `Excluded entities specified by author: ${excludedList} - Included entities specified by author: ${includedList}`
   163	        )

   173	        if (this.isBlank) return this

   176	        const adjustedStart = start === Infinity ? this.maxTime! : start
   177	        const adjustedEnd = end === -Infinity ? this.minTime! : end
   178	        // todo: we should set a time column onload so we don't have to worry about it again.
   179	        const timeColumnSlug = this.timeColumn?.slug || OwidTableSlugs.time
   180	
   181	        const description = `Keep only rows with Time between ${adjustedStart} - ${adjustedEnd}`
   182	
   183	        // perf: if the time range is greater than the table's time range, we can skip the filter
   184	        if (adjustedStart <= this.minTime && adjustedEnd >= this.maxTime!)

   186	
   187	        return this.columnFilter(

   190	                (time as number) >= adjustedStart &&
   191	                (time as number) <= adjustedEnd,

   201	        const timeValues = timeColumn.valuesIncludingErrorValues

   205	            const indices = entityNameToIndices.get(entityName) || []

   210	            targetTimes.forEach((targetTime) => {

   213	                    targetTime,

   215	                )
   216	                if (index !== undefined) matchingIndices.add(indices[index])
   217	            })
   218	        })
   219	
   220	        return this.columnFilter(

   223	            `Keep a row for each entity for each of the closest times ${targetTimes.join(
   224	                ", "
   225	            )} with tolerance ${tolerance}`

   227	    }

   259	        return this.rowFilter(
   260	            (row) => slugs.some((slug) => isNotErrorValue(row[slug])),
   261	            `Drop rows with empty or ErrorValues in every column: ${slugs.join(
   262	                ", "
   263	            )}`
   264	        )
   265	    }
   266	
   267	    // Drop _all rows_ for an entity if there is any column that has no valid values for that entity.
   268	    dropEntitiesThatHaveNoDataInSomeColumn(columnSlugs: ColumnSlug[]): this {
   269	        const indexesByEntityName = this.rowIndicesByEntityName
   270	
   271	        // Iterate over all entities, and remove them as we go if they have no data in some column
   272	        const entityNamesToKeep = new Set(indexesByEntityName.keys())
   273	
   274	        for (const slug of columnSlugs) {
   275	            const col = this.get(slug)
   276	
   277	            // Optimization, if there are no error values in this column, we can skip this column
   278	            if (col.numErrorValues === 0) continue
   279	
   280	            for (const entityName of entityNamesToKeep) {
   281	                const indicesForEntityName = indexesByEntityName.get(entityName)
   282	                if (!indicesForEntityName)
   283	                    throw new Error("Unexpected: entity not found in index map")
   284	
   285	                // Optimization: We don't care about the number of valid/error values, we just need
   286	                // to know if there is at least one valid value
   287	                const hasSomeValidValueForEntityInCol =
   288	                    indicesForEntityName.some((index) =>
   289	                        isNotErrorValue(col.valuesIncludingErrorValues[index])
   290	                    )
   291	
   292	                // Optimization: If we find a column that this entity has no data in we can remove
   293	                // it immediately, no need to iterate over other columns also
   294	                if (!hasSomeValidValueForEntityInCol)
   295	                    entityNamesToKeep.delete(entityName)
   296	            }
   297	        }
   298	
   299	        const entityNamesToDrop = differenceOfSets([
   300	            this.availableEntityNameSet,
   301	            entityNamesToKeep,
   302	        ])
   303	        const droppedEntitiesStr =
   304	            entityNamesToDrop.size > 0
   305	                ? [...entityNamesToDrop].join(", ")
   306	                : "(None)"
   307	
   308	        if (entityNamesToDrop.size === 0) {
   309	            return this.noopTransform(
   310	                `Drop entities that have no data in some column`
   311	            )
   312	        }
   313	
   314	        return this.columnFilter(
   315	            this.entityNameSlug,
   316	            (rowEntityName) => entityNamesToKeep.has(rowEntityName as string),
   317	            `Drop ${entityNamesToDrop.size} entities that have no data in some column: ${columnSlugs.join(", ")}.\nDropped entities: ${droppedEntitiesStr}`
   318	        )
   319	    }
   320	
   321	    // Drop _all rows_ for an entity if all columns have at least one invalid or missing value for that entity.
   322	    dropEntitiesThatHaveSomeMissingOrErrorValueInAllColumns(
   323	        columnSlugs: ColumnSlug[]
   324	    ): this {
   325	        const indexesByEntityName = this.rowIndicesByEntityName
   326	        const uniqTimes = new Set(this.allTimes)
   327	
   328	        // entity names to iterate over
   329	        const entityNamesToIterateOver = new Set(indexesByEntityName.keys())
   330	
   331	        // set of entities we want to keep
   332	        const entityNamesToKeep = new Set<string>()
   333	
   334	        // total number of entities
   335	        const entityCount = entityNamesToIterateOver.size
   336	
   337	        // helper function to generate operation name
   338	        const makeOpName = (entityNamesToKeep: Set<EntityName>): string => {
   339	            const entityNamesToDrop = differenceOfSets([
   340	                this.availableEntityNameSet,
   341	                entityNamesToKeep,
   342	            ])
   343	            const droppedEntitiesStr =
   344	                entityNamesToDrop.size > 0
   345	                    ? [...entityNamesToDrop].join(", ")
   346	                    : "(None)"
   347	            return `Drop entities that have some missing or error value in all column: ${columnSlugs.join(", ")}.\nDropped entities: ${droppedEntitiesStr}`
   348	        }
   349	
   350	        // Optimization: if there is a column that has a valid data entry for
   351	        // every entity and every time, we are done
   352	        for (const slug of columnSlugs) {
   353	            const col = this.get(slug)
   354	
   355	            if (
   356	                col.numValues === entityCount * uniqTimes.size &&
   357	                col.numErrorValues === 0
   358	            ) {
   359	                const entityNamesToKeep = new Set(indexesByEntityName.keys())
   360	
   361	                return this.columnFilter(
   362	                    this.entityNameSlug,
   363	                    (rowEntityName) =>
   364	                        entityNamesToKeep.has(rowEntityName as string),
   365	                    makeOpName(entityNamesToKeep)
   366	                )
   367	            }
   368	        }
   369	
   370	        for (const slug of columnSlugs) {
   371	            const col = this.get(slug)
   372	
   373	            for (const entityName of entityNamesToIterateOver) {
   374	                const indicesForEntityName = indexesByEntityName.get(entityName)
   375	                if (!indicesForEntityName)
   376	                    throw new Error("Unexpected: entity not found in index map")
   377	
   378	                // Optimization: If the column is missing values for the entity,
   379	                // we know we can't make a decision yet, so we skip this entity
   380	                if (indicesForEntityName.length < uniqTimes.size) continue
   381	
   382	                // Optimization: We don't care about the number of valid/error
   383	                // values, we just need to know if there is at least one invalid value
   384	                const hasSomeInvalidValueForEntityInCol =
   385	                    indicesForEntityName.some(
   386	                        (index) =>
   387	                            !isNotErrorValue(
   388	                                col.valuesIncludingErrorValues[index]
   389	                            )
   390	                    )
   391	
   392	                // Optimization: If all values are valid, we know we want to keep this entity,
   393	                // so we remove it from the entities to iterate over
   394	                if (!hasSomeInvalidValueForEntityInCol) {
   395	                    entityNamesToKeep.add(entityName)
   396	                    entityNamesToIterateOver.delete(entityName)
   397	                }
   398	            }
   399	        }
   400	
   401	        return this.columnFilter(
   402	            this.entityNameSlug,
   403	            (rowEntityName) => entityNamesToKeep.has(rowEntityName as string),
   404	            makeOpName(entityNamesToKeep)
   405	        )
   406	    }
   407	
   408	    private sumsByTime(columnSlug: ColumnSlug): Map<number, number> {
   409	        const timeValues = this.timeColumn.values
   410	        const values = this.get(columnSlug).values as number[]
   411	        if (timeValues.length !== values.length)
   412	            // Throwing here may seem drastic but this will lead to an error in any case if the lengths are different
   413	            // (can happen when dropping rows with errors is done incorrectly).
   414	            // When it happens then throwing here is an easier to diagnose error
   415	            throw Error(
   416	                `Tried to run sumsByTime when timeValues (${timeValues.length}) and values (${values.length}) had different length`
   417	            )
   418	        const map = new Map<number, number>()
   419	        timeValues.forEach((time, index) =>
   420	            map.set(time, (map.get(time) ?? 0) + values[index])
   421	        )
   422	        return map
   423	    }

    30	export const columnStoreToRows = (
    31	    columnStore: CoreColumnStore
    32	): Record<string, CoreValueType>[] => {
    33	    const firstCol = Object.values(columnStore)[0]
    34	    if (!firstCol) return []
    35	    const slugs = Object.keys(columnStore)
    36	    return firstCol.map((val, index) => {
    37	        const newRow: Record<string, CoreValueType> = {}
    38	        slugs.forEach((slug) => {

    42	    })

    49	// Picks a type for each column from the first row then autotypes all rows after that so all values in
    50	// a column will have the same type. Only chooses between strings and numbers.
    51	const numberOnly = /^-?\d+\.?\d*$/
    52	type RawRow = Record<string, unknown> | undefined
    53	type ParsedRow = Record<string, string | number | ErrorValue> | undefined | null
    54	export const makeAutoTypeFn = (
    55	    numericSlugs?: ColumnSlug[]
    56	): ((object?: RawRow) => ParsedRow) => {
    57	    const slugToType: any = {}
    58	    numericSlugs?.forEach((slug) => {
    59	        slugToType[slug] = "number"
    60	    })
    61	    return (object: RawRow): ParsedRow => {
    62	        for (const columnSlug in object) {
    63	            const value = object[columnSlug]
    64	            const type = slugToType[columnSlug]
    65	            if (type === "string") {
    66	                object[columnSlug] = value
    67	                continue
    68	            }
    69	
    70	            const number = parseFloat(value as string) // The "+" type casting that d3 does for perf converts "" to 0, so use parseFloat.
    71	            if (type === "number") {
    72	                object[columnSlug] = isNaN(number)
    73	                    ? ErrorValueTypes.NaNButShouldBeNumber
    74	                    : number
    75	                continue
    76	            }
    77	
    78	            if (isNaN(number) || !numberOnly.test(value as string)) {
    79	                object[columnSlug] = value
    80	                slugToType[columnSlug] = "string"
    81	                continue
    82	            }
    83	
    84	            object[columnSlug] = number
    85	            slugToType[columnSlug] = "number"
    86	        }
    87	        return object as ParsedRow
    88	    }
    89	}
    90	
    91	// Removes whitespace and non-word characters from column slugs if any exist.
    92	// The original names are moved to the name property on the column def.
    93	export const standardizeSlugs = (
    94	    rows: CoreRow[]
    95	): { rows: CoreRow[]; defs: { name: string; slug: string }[] } | undefined => {
    96	    const firstRow = rows[0] ?? {}
    97	    const colsToRename = Object.keys(firstRow)
    98	        .map((name) => {
    99	            return {
   100	                name,
   101	                slug: slugifySameCase(name),
   102	            }
   103	        })
   104	        .filter((col) => col.name !== col.slug)
   105	    if (!colsToRename.length) return undefined
   106	
   107	    rows.forEach((row: CoreRow) => {
   108	        colsToRename.forEach((col) => {
   109	            row[col.slug] = row[col.name]
   110	            delete row[col.name]
   111	        })
   112	    })
   113	
   114	    return { rows, defs: colsToRename }
   115	}
   116	
   117	export const guessColumnDefFromSlugAndRow = (
   118	    slug: string,
   119	    sampleValue: unknown
   120	): CoreColumnDef => {
   121	    const valueType = typeof sampleValue
   122	
   123	    const name = slug
   124	
   125	    if (slug === "Entity")
   126	        return {
   127	            slug,
   128	            type: ColumnTypeNames.EntityName,
   129	            name,
   130	        }
   131	
   132	    if (slug === "day")
   133	        return {
   134	            slug,
   135	            type: ColumnTypeNames.Day,
   136	            name: "Day",
   137	        }
   138	
   139	    if (slug === "year" || slug === "Year")
   140	        return {
   141	            slug,
   142	            type: ColumnTypeNames.Year,
   143	            name: "Year",
   144	        }
   145	
   146	    if (slug === OwidTableSlugs.entityName) return OwidEntityNameColumnDef
   147	    if (slug === OwidTableSlugs.entityCode) return OwidEntityCodeColumnDef
   148	    if (slug === OwidTableSlugs.entityId) return OwidEntityIdColumnDef
   149	
   150	    if (slug === "date")
   151	        return {
   152	            slug,
   153	            type: ColumnTypeNames.Date,
   154	            name: "Date",
   155	        }
   156	
   157	    if (valueType === "number")
   158	        return {
   159	            slug,
   160	            type: ColumnTypeNames.Numeric,
   161	            name,
   162	        }
   163	
   164	    if (valueType === "string") {
   165	        if (String(sampleValue).match(/^\d+$/))
   166	            return {
   167	                slug,
   168	                type: ColumnTypeNames.Numeric,
   169	                name,
   170	            }
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    return { slug, type: ColumnTypeNames.String, name }
   174	}
   175	
   176	export const makeRowFromColumnStore = (
   177	    rowIndex: number,
   178	    columnStore: CoreColumnStore
   179	): CoreRow => {
   180	    const row: CoreRow = {}
   181	    Object.entries(columnStore).forEach(([slug, col]) => {
   182	        if (col.length <= rowIndex) row[slug] = undefined
   183	        else row[slug] = col[rowIndex]
   184	    })
   185	    return row
   186	}
   187	
   188	// eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-empty-interface, @typescript-eslint/no-empty-object-type
   189	export interface InterpolationContext {}
   190	
   191	export interface LinearInterpolationContext extends InterpolationContext {
   192	    // whether to extrapolate a variable at the start or end, where we cannot do linear interpolation
   193	    // but need to just copy over the first/last value present over to empty fields.
   194	    // e.g. [Error, Error, 2, 3, 4] would become [2, 2, 2, 3, 4] with extrapolateAtStart=true.
   195	    extrapolateAtStart?: boolean
   196	    extrapolateAtEnd?: boolean
   197	}
   198	
   199	export interface ToleranceInterpolationContext extends InterpolationContext {
   200	    timeToleranceForwards: number
   201	    timeToleranceBackwards: number
   202	}
   203	
   204	export type InterpolationProvider<C extends InterpolationContext> = (
   205	    valuesSortedByTimeAsc: (number | ErrorValue)[],
   206	    timesAsc: Time[],
   207	    context: C,
   208	    start: number,
   209	    end: number
   210	) => void
   211	
   212	export function linearInterpolation(
   213	    valuesSortedByTimeAsc: (number | ErrorValue)[],
   214	    timesAsc: Time[],
   215	    context: LinearInterpolationContext,
   216	    start: number = 0,
   217	    end: number = valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length
   218	): void {
   219	    if (!valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length) return
   220	
   221	    let prevNonBlankIndex = -1
   222	    let nextNonBlankIndex = -1
   223	
   224	    for (let index = start; index < end; index++) {
   225	        const currentValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index]
   226	        if (isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(currentValue)) {
   227	            prevNonBlankIndex = index
   228	            continue
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        if (nextNonBlankIndex === -1 || nextNonBlankIndex <= index) {
   232	            nextNonBlankIndex = findIndexFast(
   233	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc,
   234	                (val) => isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(val),
   235	                index + 1,
   236	                end
   237	            )
   238	        }
   239	
   240	        const prevValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[prevNonBlankIndex]
   241	        const nextValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[nextNonBlankIndex]
   242	
   243	        let value
   244	        if (
   245	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(prevValue) &&
   246	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(nextValue)
   247	        ) {
   248	            const distLeft = index - prevNonBlankIndex
   249	            const distRight = nextNonBlankIndex - index
   250	            value =
   251	                (prevValue * distRight + nextValue * distLeft) /
   252	                (distLeft + distRight)
   253	        } else if (
   254	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(prevValue) &&
   255	            context.extrapolateAtEnd
   256	        )
   257	            value = prevValue
   258	        else if (
   259	            isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(nextValue) &&
   260	            context.extrapolateAtStart
   261	        )
   262	            value = nextValue
   263	        else value = ErrorValueTypes.NoValueForInterpolation
   264	
   265	        prevNonBlankIndex = index
   266	
   267	        valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] = value
   268	    }
   269	}
   270	
   271	export function toleranceInterpolation(
   272	    valuesSortedByTimeAsc: (number | ErrorValue)[],
   273	    timesAsc: Time[],
   274	    context: ToleranceInterpolationContext,
   275	    start: number = 0,
   276	    end: number = valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length
   277	): void {
   278	    if (!valuesSortedByTimeAsc.length) return
   279	
   280	    let prevNonBlankIndex: number | undefined = undefined
   281	    let nextNonBlankIndex: number | undefined = undefined
   282	
   283	    for (let index = start; index < end; index++) {
   284	        const currentValue = valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index]
   285	        if (isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell(currentValue)) {
   286	            prevNonBlankIndex = index
   287	            continue
   288	        }
   289	
   290	        if (
   291	            context.timeToleranceForwards > 0 &&
   292	            nextNonBlankIndex !== -1 &&
   293	            (nextNonBlankIndex === undefined || nextNonBlankIndex <= index)
   294	        ) {
   295	            nextNonBlankIndex = findIndexFast(
   296	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc,
   297	                isNotErrorValueOrEmptyCell,
   298	                index + 1,
   299	                end
   300	            )
   301	        }
   302	
   303	        const timeOfCurrent = timesAsc[index]
   304	        const timeOfPrevIndex =
   305	            prevNonBlankIndex !== undefined
   306	                ? timesAsc[prevNonBlankIndex]
   307	                : -Infinity
   308	        const timeOfNextIndex =
   309	            nextNonBlankIndex !== undefined && nextNonBlankIndex !== -1
   310	                ? timesAsc[nextNonBlankIndex]
   311	                : Infinity
   312	
   313	        const prevTimeDiff = Math.abs(timeOfPrevIndex - timeOfCurrent)
   314	        const nextTimeDiff = Math.abs(timeOfNextIndex - timeOfCurrent)
   315	
   316	        if (
   317	            nextNonBlankIndex !== -1 &&
   318	            nextTimeDiff <= prevTimeDiff &&
   319	            nextTimeDiff <= context.timeToleranceForwards
   320	        ) {
   321	            valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] =
   322	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc[nextNonBlankIndex!]
   323	            timesAsc[index] = timesAsc[nextNonBlankIndex!]
   324	        } else if (
   325	            prevNonBlankIndex !== undefined &&
   326	            prevTimeDiff <= context.timeToleranceBackwards
   327	        ) {
   328	            valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] =
   329	                valuesSortedByTimeAsc[prevNonBlankIndex!]
   330	            timesAsc[index] = timesAsc[prevNonBlankIndex!]
   331	        } else
   332	            valuesSortedByTimeAsc[index] =
   333	                ErrorValueTypes.NoValueWithinTolerance
   334	    }
   335	}
   336	
   337	// A dumb function for making a function that makes a key for a row given certain columns.
   338	export const makeKeyFn = (
   339	    columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   340	    columnSlugs: ColumnSlug[]
   341	): ((rowIndex: number) => string) => {
   342	    const cols = columnSlugs.map((slug) => columnStore[slug])
   343	
   344	    const toStr = (val: CoreValueType): string =>
   345	        val === null || val === undefined
   346	            ? ""
   347	            : typeof val === "string"
   348	              ? val
   349	              : (val as any) + ""
   350	
   351	    // perf: this function is performance-critical, and so for the common cases of 1, 2, or 3 columns, we can provide a
   352	    // faster implementation.
   353	    if (cols.length === 0) return () => ""
   354	    if (cols.length === 1) {
   355	        const col = cols[0]
   356	        return (rowIndex: number): string => toStr(col[rowIndex])
   357	    }
   358	    if (cols.length === 2) {
   359	        const col0 = cols[0],
   360	            col1 = cols[1]
   361	        return (rowIndex: number): string =>
   362	            `${toStr(col0[rowIndex])} ${toStr(col1[rowIndex])}`
   363	    }
   364	    if (cols.length === 3) {
   365	        const col0 = cols[0],
   366	            col1 = cols[1],
   367	            col2 = cols[2]
   368	        return (rowIndex: number): string =>
   369	            `${toStr(col0[rowIndex])} ${toStr(col1[rowIndex])} ${toStr(
   370	                col2[rowIndex]
   371	            )}`
   372	    }
   373	
   374	    return (rowIndex: number): string =>
   375	        // toString() handles `undefined` and `null` values, which can be in the table.
   376	        cols.map((col) => toStr(col[rowIndex])).join(" ")
   377	}
   378	
   379	const getColumnStoreLength = (store: CoreColumnStore): number => {
   380	    return _.max(Object.values(store).map((v) => v.length)) ?? 0
   381	}
   382	
   383	export const concatColumnStores = (
   384	    stores: CoreColumnStore[],
   385	    slugsToKeep?: ColumnSlug[]
   386	): CoreColumnStore => {
   387	    if (!stores.length) return {}
   388	
   389	    const lengths = stores.map(getColumnStoreLength)
   390	    const slugs = slugsToKeep ?? Object.keys(R.first(stores)!)
   391	
   392	    const newColumnStore: CoreColumnStore = {}
   393	
   394	    // The below code is performance-critical.
   395	    // That's why it's written using for loops and mutable arrays rather than using map or flatMap:
   396	    // To this day, that's still faster in JS.
   397	    slugs.forEach((slug) => {
   398	        let newColumnValues: CoreValueType[] = []
   399	        for (const [i, store] of stores.entries()) {
   400	            const values = store[slug] ?? []
   401	            const toFill = Math.max(0, lengths[i] - values.length)
   402	
   403	            newColumnValues = newColumnValues.concat(values)
   404	            if (toFill > 0) {
   405	                newColumnValues = newColumnValues.concat(
   406	                    new Array(toFill).fill(
   407	                        ErrorValueTypes.MissingValuePlaceholder
   408	                    )
   409	                )
   410	            }
   411	        }
   412	        newColumnStore[slug] = newColumnValues
   413	    })
   414	    return newColumnStore
   415	}
   416	
   417	export const rowsToColumnStore = (rows: CoreRow[]): CoreColumnStore => {
   418	    const columnsObject: CoreColumnStore = {}
   419	    if (!rows.length) return columnsObject
   420	
   421	    Object.keys(rows[0]).forEach((slug) => {
   422	        columnsObject[slug] = rows.map((row) => row[slug])
   423	    })
   424	    return columnsObject
   425	}
   426	
   427	const guessColumnDefsFromRows = (
   428	    rows: CoreRow[],
   429	    definedSlugs: Map<ColumnSlug, any>
   430	): CoreColumnDef[] => {
   431	    if (!rows[0]) return []
   432	    return Object.keys(rows[0])
   433	        .filter((slug) => !definedSlugs.has(slug))
   434	        .map((slug) => {
   435	            const firstRowWithValue = rows.find(
   436	                (row) =>
   437	                    row[slug] !== undefined &&
   438	                    row[slug] !== null &&
   439	                    row[slug] !== ""
   440	            )
   441	            const firstValue = firstRowWithValue
   442	                ? firstRowWithValue[slug]
   443	                : undefined
   444	
   445	            return guessColumnDefFromSlugAndRow(slug, firstValue)
   446	        })
   447	}
   448	
   449	export const autodetectColumnDefs = (
   450	    rowsOrColumnStore: CoreColumnStore | CoreRow[],
   451	    definedSlugs: Map<ColumnSlug, any>
   452	): CoreColumnDef[] => {
   453	    if (!Array.isArray(rowsOrColumnStore)) {
   454	        const columnStore = rowsOrColumnStore as CoreColumnStore
   455	        return Object.keys(columnStore)
   456	            .filter((slug) => !definedSlugs.has(slug))
   457	            .map((slug) => {
   458	                return guessColumnDefFromSlugAndRow(
   459	                    slug,
   460	                    columnStore[slug].find(
   461	                        (val) => val !== undefined && val !== null
   462	                    )
   463	                )
   464	            })
   465	    }
   466	    return guessColumnDefsFromRows(rowsOrColumnStore, definedSlugs)
   467	}
   468	
   469	// Convenience method when you are replacing columns
   470	export const replaceDef = <ColumnDef extends CoreColumnDef>(
   471	    defs: ColumnDef[],
   472	    newDefs: ColumnDef[]
   473	): ColumnDef[] =>
   474	    defs.map((def) => {
   475	        const newDef = newDefs.find((newDef) => newDef.slug === def.slug)
   476	        return newDef ?? def
   477	    })
   478	
   479	export const renameColumnStore = (
   480	    columnStore: CoreColumnStore,
   481	    columnRenameMap: { [columnSlug: string]: ColumnSlug }
   482	): CoreColumnStore => {
   483	    const newStore: CoreColumnStore = {}
   484	    Object.keys(columnStore).forEach((slug) => {
   485	        if (columnRenameMap[slug])
   486	            newStore[columnRenameMap[slug]] = columnStore[slug]
   487	        else newStore[slug] = columnStore[slug]
   488	    })
   489	    return newStore
   490	}

   492	// Returns a Set of random indexes to drop in an array, preserving the order of the array
   493	export const getDropIndexes = (
   494	    arrayLength: number,
   495	    howMany: number,
   496	    seed = Date.now()
   497	): Set<number> => new Set(sampleFrom(_.range(0, arrayLength), howMany, seed))

    64	describe(withUniformSpacing, () => {
    65	    it("can add values to make an array evenly spaced", () => {
    66	        expect(withUniformSpacing([])).toEqual([])
    67	        expect(withUniformSpacing([5])).toEqual([5])

    72	            1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7, 8,
    73	        ])
    74	        expect(withUniformSpacing([7, 12, 17])).toEqual([7, 12, 17])
    75	    })
    76	})

    78	describe(withMissingValuesAsZeroes, () => {

     1	/**
     2	 * Previously when we get a blank for a value, or a string where we expect a number, etc,
     3	 * we parse things as simply undefineds or nulls or NaN. Since authors are uploading data
     4	 * from our sources at runtime, and errors in source data are extremely common, it may be helpful
     5	 * to parse those invalid values into specific types, to provide better error message and perhaps
     6	 * in the future suggested autocorrections or workarounds.
     7	 *
     8	 * For a good read on the "Errors are values" pattern: https://blog.golang.org/errors-are-values
     9	 */
    10

    62	export const isNotErrorValue = <TYPE>(item: TYPE | ErrorValue): item is TYPE =>
    63	    !(item instanceof ErrorValue)
    64

    66	    value: K
